Generalizes `recoverableByDepth_scheme` (rank-2 only) to every P-polynomial schurian scheme graph тАФ cycles, Johnson, Hamming, all DRGs тАФ in one oracle-vocabulary export; depth-1 cells non-singleton (genuine recovery at the structural oracle's node). | тАФ |
| `recoverableByDepth_univ` | 857-864 | Every graph is trivially recoverable by depth `n` (individualize everything), so only the *polynomial* depth bound is cascade-class content. | тАФ |
| `CascadeComplete` | 871-878 | Completeness contract: the oracle certifies every genuine `Aut_D`-orbit pair; with soundness it then computes the orbit relation exactly. | Definition |
| `certifies_iff_orbit` | 880-894 | For a sound and complete cascade oracle, it returns `some` exactly on the pairs sharing an `Aut_D`-orbit. | тАФ |
| `CellComplete` | 896-903 | The polynomial completeness contract: the oracle certifies every pair sharing a 1-WL cell (refinement-decidable). | Definition |
| `complete_of_cellComplete_recoverable` | 905-918 | **Key theorem.** At an orbit-recoverable node, certifying every same-cell pair already certifies every orbit тАФ reducing orbit-completeness to a polynomial check. | тАФ |
| `VerdictIsoInvariant` | 965-978 | Iso-invariance contract (strategy ┬з15 gap 2): the oracle's verdict depends only on the iso-invariant 1-WL partition. Derivable тАФ see `verdictIsoInvariant_of_complete`. | Definition |
| `cascadeComplete_of_localization` | 980-991 | Capstone: cell-completeness plus all-nodes recoverability yields `CascadeComplete`, naming the open localisation obligation as its hypotheses. | тАФ |
| `cascadeComplete_of_cellsAreOrbits` | 993-1004 | Capstone stated against the single open implication: cell-completeness plus `CellsAreOrbits` at every node yields `CascadeComplete`. | тАФ |
| `verdictIsoInvariant_of_complete` | 1006-1021 | **Key theorem.** A sound, complete oracle at orbit-recoverable nodes is automatically iso-invariant, so iso-invariance is part of localisation rather than a separate obligation. | тАФ |
| `computes_orbits_of_complete` | 1023-1035 | Capstone: a sound and complete cascade oracle computes the `Aut_D`-orbit relation exactly (program-level correctness, given the completeness obligation). | тАФ |

| `rankPerm_inv_mul_eq_of_match` | 1052-1064 | ┬зC.4 M-B тАФ the rank-composition identity behind `colourMatchPerm = g`: if `g` value-matches the two colourings (`╧ЗтВВ тИШ g = ╧ЗтВБ`), then `(rankPerm ╧ЗтВВ)тБ╗┬╣ * rankPerm ╧ЗтВБ = g`. Pure `vertexRank_comp` reindexing, no graph structure. | тАФ |
| `colourMatchPerm` | 1066-1076 | ┬зC.4 **M-B тАФ the colour-match permutation.** The explicit `Equiv.Perm` from the two *discrete* branch colourings, as the rank composition `(rankPerm ╧З_w)тБ╗┬╣ * (rankPerm ╧З_v)` (`╧З_r = warmRefine adj P (indivWithRep n D r)`). Always well-defined given discreteness; `= g` at a recoverable node. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `colourMatchPerm_eq_of_orbit` | 1078-1091 | ┬зC.4 **M-B completeness linchpin.** An `Aut_D` witness `g` (`g v = w`, `w тИЙ D`) value-matches the two branch colourings (`colourMatch_complete`), so `colourMatchPerm = g` тАФ built from the colours, not assumed. | тАФ |
| `matchOracle` | 1092-1110 | ┬зC.4 **M-B тАФ the colour-match cascade oracle.** Constructs `colourMatchPerm` (when both footprints discrete) and returns it **iff** it verifies as an `Aut_D` orbit map (`IsAut тИз P-preserving тИз fixes D тИз v тЖж w`). Construct-and-check, not the existential shortcut. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `matchOracle_orbitMapSpec` | 1135-1145 | ┬зC.4 **M-B soundness тАФ `OrbitMapSpec`, unconditional.** When `matchOracle` fires, its four checks *are* the `OrbitPartition` witness conditions, so the returned perm certifies a genuine `Aut_D` orbit pair. No discreteness/recoverability hypothesis. | тАФ |
| `matchOracle_cellComplete` | 1147-1183 | ┬зC.4 **M-B completeness тАФ `CellComplete`.** Conditional on every node one-step-discretizing (`hdisc`, = the exposure-depth witness / M-C / "B's core") and `CellsAreOrbits` everywhere (`hco`, = localisation): at a same-cell pair the orbit automorphism exists, `colourMatchPerm = g`, so the oracle fires. | тАФ |
| `matchOracle_cascadeComplete` | 1185-1196 | ┬зC.4 **M-B capstone тАФ `CascadeComplete`.** `matchOracle` computes the orbit relation exactly, reduced to the two named-open hypotheses (discretizing depth + `CellsAreOrbits`); soundness is already unconditional. | тАФ |
| `matchOracle_verdictIsoInvariant` | 1198-1212 | ┬зC.4 **M-B тАФ flag iso-invariance, free.** With soundness + completeness, `verdictIsoInvariant_of_complete` gives the verdict as a function of the iso-invariant 1-WL partition (strategy ┬з15 gap 2) for `matchOracle` on the recoverable class. | тАФ |
| `discrete_of_samePartition` | 1231-1234 | ┬зC.4b Discreteness transfers across `samePartition`: `samePartition ╧ЗтВБ ╧ЗтВВ тЖТ Discrete ╧ЗтВБ тЖТ Discrete ╧ЗтВВ`. | тАФ |
| `warmRefine_samePartition` | 1236-1241 | ┬зC.4b `warmRefine` respects `samePartition` (specialization of `warmRefine_agree_off'`, `D = тИЕ`): equal-partition starts warm-refine to equal-partition results. | тАФ |
| `samePartition_indivWithRep_insert` | 1243-1284 | ┬зC.4b **Single-rep footprint = indexed `insert`.** For `r тИЙ D`, `indivWithRep n D r` and `individualizedColouring n (insert r D)` induce the same partition (`r` globally unique either way). | тАФ |
| `discrete_indivWithRep_of_discrete_insert` | 1286-1295 | ┬зC.4b **The M-B depth-witness bridge.** M-B's `hdisc` follows from discreteness of the *indexed* `individualizedColouring (insert r D)` тАФ connecting the depth witness to the `RecoverableByDepth` framework, class-agnostically. | тАФ |
| `indivWithSet` | 1312-1317 | ┬зC.5 **M-C тАФ multi-step uniform individualization.** Individualize the committed set `S` by index, plus an explored *set* `R` with a single uniform fresh colour `n+1`. Generalizes `indivWithRep` (`R = {r}`); uniform on `R` is forced by transport (an orbit aut moves `R`). | Definition |
| `indivWithRep_eq_indivWithSet` | 1319-1322 | ┬зC.5 `indivWithRep n S r = indivWithSet n S {r}` тАФ the singleton bridge to M-B. | тАФ |
| `indivWithSet_transport` | 1324-1343 | ┬зC.5 **M-C transport.** An orbit aut `g` fixing `S` with `RтВВ = RтВБ.image g` carries the branch-`RтВБ` colouring onto branch-`RтВВ` (`╧ЗтВВ тИШ g = ╧ЗтВБ`); the `indivWithRep_transport` generalization (uniform colour on the moved set is what makes it hold). | тАФ |
| `IsColourMatchSet` | 1345-1349 | ┬зC.5 The multi-step colour-match relation: `t` matches branch-`RтВВ`'s refined colours to branch-`RтВБ`'s. The `IsColourMatch` generalization. | Definition |
| `colourMatchSet_complete` | 1351-1358 | ┬зC.5 **M-C completeness brick.** The orbit aut `g` (fixing `S`, `RтВВ = RтВБ.image g`) *is* a colour-match (`warmRefine_transport тИШ indivWithSet_transport`). | тАФ |
| `colourMatchSet_unique` | 1360-1370 | ┬зC.5 **M-C uniqueness brick.** At a discrete branch-`RтВВ` footprint any colour-match `= g`, via the colouring-generic `colourMatch_eq_aut`. | тАФ |
| `harvestSet_isAut_of_discrete` | 1372-1382 | ┬зC.5 **M-C harvest brick.** At a discrete branch-`RтВВ` footprint the colour-match candidate verifies (`= g`) тАФ the harvest now fires at a footprint discretized by an explored *set* (a sequence), not just one rep. | тАФ |
| `colourMatchPermSet` | 1384-1391 | ┬зC.5 **M-C тАФ the multi-step colour-match permutation.** The rank composition `(rankPerm ╧З_{RтВВ})тБ╗┬╣ * (rankPerm ╧З_{RтВБ})` for set footprints; `colourMatchPerm` is the `RтВБ={v}, RтВВ={w}` case. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `colourMatchPermSet_eq_of_orbit` | 1393-1403 | ┬зC.5 `colourMatchPermSet = g` at a recoverable set-footprint (`rankPerm_inv_mul_eq_of_match` тЖР `vertexRank_comp` + `colourMatchSet_complete`); the multi-step `colourMatchPerm_eq_of_orbit`. | тАФ |
| `colourMatchSet_exists_of_cellsAreOrbits` | 1405-1418 | ┬зC.5 **The multi-step firing certificate exists.** From `CellsAreOrbits` at a same-cell pair, for *any* exploration set `RтВБ` the orbit aut `g`, partner `RтВВ = RтВБ.image g`, and the colour-match all exist. The open piece (M-D) is that the oracle's branch-`w` set *is* `RтВБ.image g` (lockstep). | тАФ |
| `matchOracleSet` | 1431-1451 | ┬зC.6 **M-D тАФ the multi-step colour-match oracle.** Like `matchOracle` but individualizes a whole explored *set* `expand chain r` (per an exploration selector) on top of the committed path; constructs `colourMatchPermSet`, returns it **iff** it verifies `IsAut тИз P-preserving тИз fixes D тИз v тЖж w`. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `matchOracleSet_orbitMapSpec` | 1480-1490 | ┬зC.6 **M-D soundness тАФ `OrbitMapSpec`, unconditional.** When it fires the four checks *are* the `OrbitPartition` witness; no discreteness/recoverability/lockstep hypothesis. | тАФ |
| `LockstepExpand` | 1492-1502 | ┬зC.6 **The lockstep correspondence** as equivariance of the exploration rule: any `P`-preserving automorphism fixing the committed path carries one branch's exploration set onto the other's (`expand chain (g v) = (expand chain v).image g`). Discharged for `forcedExpand` (`Cascade.lean`). | Definition |
| `matchOracleSet_cellComplete` | 1504-1544 | ┬зC.6 **M-D completeness тАФ `CellComplete`.** Reduced to set-footprint discreteness (the multi-step depth witness) + `CellsAreOrbits` + `LockstepExpand`: the lockstep supplies `RтВВ = RтВБ.image g`, so `colourMatchPermSet = g` and the oracle fires. | тАФ |
| `matchOracleSet_cascadeComplete` | 1546-1558 | ┬зC.6 **M-D capstone тАФ `CascadeComplete`** (the multi-step oracle computes the orbit relation exactly), reduced to the three named-open hypotheses. | тАФ |
| `matchOracleSet_verdictIsoInvariant` | 1560-1573 | ┬зC.6 **M-D тАФ flag iso-invariance, free** (via `verdictIsoInvariant_of_complete`). | тАФ |
| `matchOracle_fires_of_insertDiscrete` | 1606-1629 | ┬зC.7 **Honest per-node firing (`hco`-free).** At a node where committing the path plus the query rep discretizes (the indexed `RecoverableByDepth` form, bridged by ┬зC.4b), `matchOracle` fires on **any** genuine `Aut_D` orbit pair `(v,w)` (`v,w тИЙ D`) тАФ the orbit witness is consumed directly, so no `CellsAreOrbits`. | тАФ |
| `matchOracle_orbit_of_fire_mono` | 1631-1645 | ┬зC.7 **Propagate via `mono`.** A merge certified at a node holds at every shallower committed set `S тКЖ chain.D` (`OrbitPartition.mono`) тАФ the "fire deep, prune shallow" step. | тАФ |
| `matchOracle_certifies_iff_orbit_of_insertDiscrete` | 1647-1673 | ┬зC.7 **Exact orbit decider at the discretizing depth.** At a footprint-discretizing node, `matchOracle` fires on `(v,w)` **iff** they are a genuine `Aut_D` orbit pair (`hco`-free). Limits: holds only under the discreteness hypotheses (cascade depth), and decides the *path-fixing* `Aut_D`, not global `Aut`. | тАФ |
| `indivWithSeq` | 1694-1699 | ┬зC.8 **Level-coloured exploration sequence (Leg 1).** Committed `S` by index plus the `i`-th element of `rs` by its *position* colour `n+1+i`; the position colouring (not vertex index) is what transports under an orbit automorphism. | Definition |
| `samePartition_indivWithSeq` | 1710-1778 | ┬зC.8 **A1: level-coloured sequence = indexed union.** `indivWithSeq n S rs` and the indexed `individualizedColouring n (S тИк rs.toFinset)` induce the same partition (each `rs`-vertex globally unique); unconditional. | тАФ |
| `discrete_indivWithSeq_of_discrete_union` | 1780-1791 | ┬зC.8 **The Leg-1 depth-witness bridge (sequence).** Sequence-footprint discreteness follows from discreteness of the indexed `individualizedColouring n (S тИк rs.toFinset)`, so `hdiscSeq тЯ╕ recoverableByDepth`. Sequence generalization of `discrete_indivWithRep_of_discrete_insert`. | тАФ |
| `idxOf_map_of_injective` | 1805-1817 | ┬зC.8 **Position preserved by `map`.** `(l.map g).idxOf (g a) = l.idxOf a` for a permutation `g` тАФ the pure-list core of sequence transport. | тАФ |
| `indivWithSeq_transport` | 1819-1840 | ┬зC.8 **A2 transport.** An orbit aut `g` fixing `S` with `rsтВВ = rsтВБ.map g` carries the branch-`rsтВБ` level colouring onto branch-`rsтВВ` (`╧ЗтВВ тИШ g = ╧ЗтВБ`) тАФ position via `idxOf_map_of_injective`, off-sequence via `individualizedColouring` invariance. | тАФ |
| `IsColourMatchSeq` | 1842-1845 | ┬зC.8 The sequence colour-match relation (`IsColourMatchSet` analogue): `t` matches branch-`rsтВВ`'s refined colours to branch-`rsтВБ`'s. | Definition |
| `colourMatchSeq_complete` | 1847-1854 | ┬зC.8 **Sequence completeness brick.** The orbit aut `g` (fixing `S`, `rsтВВ = rsтВБ.map g`) *is* a colour-match (`warmRefine_transport тИШ indivWithSeq_transport`). | тАФ |
| `colourMatchPermSeq` | 1856-1863 | ┬зC.8 **The sequence colour-match permutation.** Rank composition `(rankPerm ╧З_{rsтВВ})тБ╗┬╣ * rankPerm ╧З_{rsтВБ}` for level-coloured footprints; `colourMatchPermSet` with the uniform set replaced by the sequence. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `colourMatchSeq_exists_of_cellsAreOrbits` | 1877-1890 | ┬зC.8 **The level-coloured firing certificate exists.** From `CellsAreOrbits`, for any sequence `rsтВБ` the orbit aut `g`, partner `rsтВВ = rsтВБ.map g`, and the colour-match exist. The open piece is the ordered lockstep (A2b). | тАФ |
| `matchOracleSeq` | 1903-1923 | ┬зC.8 **The multi-step sequence colour-match oracle.** Like `matchOracleSet` but individualizes the ordered sequence `expand chain r` via `indivWithSeq` (so its depth witness is A1-reducible); construct-and-check on `colourMatchPermSeq`. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `matchOracleSeq_orbitMapSpec` | 1951-1960 | ┬зC.8 **Sequence soundness тАФ `OrbitMapSpec`, unconditional.** When it fires the four checks *are* the `OrbitPartition` witness. | тАФ |
| `LockstepExpandSeq` | 1962-1973 | ┬зC.8 **The sequence lockstep.** The ordered (`map`, not `image`) `LockstepExpand` analogue: `expand chain (g v) = (expand chain v).map g`. Strictly stronger than the set lockstep; provably false in the multi-step regime (`lockstep_disc_imp_stab_trivial`). | Definition |
| `matchOracleSeq_cellComplete` | 1975-2014 | ┬зC.8 **Sequence completeness тАФ `CellComplete`.** Reduced to `hdiscSeq` (A1-reducible) + `hco` + `LockstepExpandSeq`. | тАФ |
| `matchOracleSeq_cascadeComplete` | 2016-2028 | ┬зC.8 **Sequence capstone тАФ `CascadeComplete`**, reduced to the same three hypotheses (the last jointly unsatisfiable with `hdiscSeq` for multi-step тАФ see `lockstep_disc_imp_stab_trivial`). | тАФ |
| `matchOracleSeq_verdictIsoInvariant` | 2030-2043 | ┬зC.8 **Sequence flag iso-invariance, free** (via `verdictIsoInvariant_of_complete`). | тАФ |
| `lockstep_disc_imp_stab_trivial` | 2075-2109 | ┬зC.8 **The discretizing-oracle limit (conservation of obstruction).** `LockstepExpandSeq тИз hdiscSeq тЯ╣ stab_{Aut_D}(v) = 1`: the sequence oracle's completeness hypotheses hold jointly only in the single-rep regime, so the discretizing colour-match cannot harvest a multi-step moved orbit (тЖТ cross-branch / SchreierтАУSims). | тАФ |
## ChainDescent/LinearOracle.lean

The linear-oracle / abelian-stripping work (tractable-buildout B2; plan + status in `docs/chain-descent-linear-oracle.md` ┬з8.2). Built on the ┬з15.8 scaffolding (`DirAssignment`/`flipPair`/`LinearOracleSpec`/`LeafTwistSpec`/`canonAdj`). Builds axiom-clean (`refineStep`/`refineStep_iff` + foundationals), no `sorry`. **B2 soundness core DONE 2026-05-30:** ┬зL.1 soundness anchor, ┬зL.2 the *forced* candidate twist (rank rebasing тАФ the construction is determined, not searched; the `canonAdj_rebase` bridge), ┬зL.3 abelian `ZтВВ^d` structure. Remaining: `canonForm` lex-min tie (needs descent-with-pruning model), completeness, lifting twists to subgroup `N` (Part A).

### ┬зL.1 тАФ Soundness anchor (B2.1)

| Name | Line | Description | Notes |
|------|------|-------------|-------|
| `RealizesFlip` | 52-61 | **Soundness anchor.** The relation "twist `t` relabels branch `╧Г`'s leaf to the flipped branch `flipPair ╧Г a b`'s leaf" тАФ the `LeafTwistSpec` conclusion with the partner branch pinned to the flip, i.e. the pruning justification. | Definition |
| `TwistWitness` | 63-83 | The verified data a twist discovery returns: the decided pair `(a,b)`, the candidate permutation `t`, its `IsAut` proof (the ┬з4.5 edge-check, sole soundness anchor), and a `RealizesFlip` proof. | Structure |
| `twistOracle` | 85-95 | A concrete `LinearOracleSpec` parameterised by an abstracted `discover` function (C#-side canonical-id matching); returns the verified automorphism from a `TwistWitness`, `none` otherwise. Verification lives inside the witness, so every output is a genuine automorphism. | Definition |
| `twistOracle_leafTwist` | 97-116 | **Key theorem (B2.1 discharge).** `twistOracle` satisfies `LeafTwistSpec`, with the flipped branch as the explicit witness `╧Г' = flipPair ╧Г` (sharper than the bare existential) тАФ closing the pruning-justification contract for any sound discovery. | тАФ |

### ┬зL.2 тАФ The forced candidate twist (B2.2 + most of B2.3)

| Name | Line | Description | Notes |
|------|------|-------------|-------|
| `canonAdj_rebase` | 159-174 | **The rebasing bridge.** Relabelling `╧Г`'s canonical leaf by the rank rebasing `rankPerm ╧А_{╧Г'} * (rankPerm ╧А_╧Г)тБ╗┬╣` yields `╧Г'`'s leaf; the flip is the `╧Г' = flipPair ╧Г` instance. | тАФ |
| `candidateTwist` | 184-192 | **The forced candidate twist** for decision `(a,b)`: the rank rebasing `rankPerm ╧А_flip * (rankPerm ╧А_╧Г)тБ╗┬╣`. Always realises the flip; the twist is determined, not searched. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `candidateTwist_realizesFlip` | 194-201 | The forced candidate always realises the flip тАФ the construction is forced, with no ambiguity. | тАФ |
| `candidateTwist_unique` | 203-215 | **Determinacy.** The candidate is the unique permutation rank-aligning `╧Г` to the flipped branch тАФ the leaf-level iso-invariance gate, making twist discovery deterministic in iso-invariant rank data. | тАФ |
| `twistWitness_of_isAut` | 217-234 | The oracle reduces to one check: a verified-automorphism forced candidate yields a complete `TwistWitness`. Discovery is a single decidable edge-check. | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `canonicalTwistOracle` | 235-249 | **The canonical twist oracle.** A fully concrete `LinearOracleSpec`: for the selected pair, compute the forced candidate and return it iff it verifies as an automorphism. The only abstracted piece is pair selection (soundness-irrelevant). | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `canonicalTwistOracle_leafTwist` | 251-259 | **Key theorem.** `canonicalTwistOracle` satisfies `LeafTwistSpec` (it is a `twistOracle`) тАФ a concrete verified linear oracle, sound by construction. | тАФ |

### ┬зL.3 тАФ Abelian structure (B2.4, partial)

| Name | Line | Description | Notes |
|------|------|-------------|-------|
| `candidateTwist_flip_inv` | 282-291 | **`ZтВВ` involution.** The forced candidate for the flip-back is the inverse of the candidate for the flip; with `flipPair_comm` this is the elementary-abelian `ZтВВ^d` structure of the residual. | тАФ |

### ┬зL.4 тАФ Completeness / effectiveness (when the oracle fires)

Characterizes *when* the oracle fires and proves firing is semantically justified. The
oracle is complete exactly on the **abelian regime** (forced candidate тИИ Aut) тАФ the
calculator ┬з6 boundary; the general converse fails (conjugation gap). The
abelian-sufficiency lemma (forced candidate IsAut for genuine abelian flips, via
`warm_6_2` rank machinery) is the open core scoped in the ┬зL.4 doc-comment.

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `isAut_candidateTwist_iff_aligned` | 329-344 | **Firing characterisation.** The forced candidate is an automorphism iff some automorphism is rank-aligned (`g ┬╖ ╧А_╧Г = ╧А_flip`) тАФ so the whole completeness question is "does a rank-aligned automorphism exist?" | тАФ |
| `RealizableFlip` | 346-352 | The decision is a genuine `Aut(adj)` symmetry: some automorphism realises the flip (the two branches are isomorphic) тАФ what pruning should require. | Definition |
| `realizableFlip_of_isAut_candidateTwist` | 354-365 | **Firing is semantically justified.** When the forced candidate verifies, the branches are genuinely `Aut(adj)`-equivalent (the candidate is the witness) тАФ pruning reflects a real symmetry. | тАФ |
| `canonicalTwistOracle_isSome_iff` | 367-383 | **Key theorem.** Given the pair selector returns `(a,b)`, the oracle fires iff the forced candidate is an automorphism тАФ the entire completeness question is one decidable edge-check. | тАФ |
| `candidateTwist_flipBack_isAut` | 385-396 | **`ZтВВ`-direction consistency.** If the forced candidate for `╧Г тЖТ flip` verifies, so does the candidate for the flip-back тАФ the oracle prunes both directions of a genuine `ZтВВ` decision consistently. | тАФ |

### ┬зL.5 тАФ Toward abelian sufficiency (partial)

The open core of completeness тАФ *forced candidate тИИ Aut for abelian decisions* тАФ needs
gadget-level rank-alignment (at a leaf both branches are discrete, so `warm_6_2`'s
partition equality is vacuous; the content is in the rank order). Provable progress:

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `candidateTwist_eq_one_of_rankPerm_eq` | 424-435 | **Absorbed decision.** Equal leaf rank permutations force the candidate to be the identity тАФ the degenerate end of the abelian regime. | тАФ |

### ┬зL.7 тАФ The CFI bridge (M1b): candidate as a conjugate of a graph automorphism

Now that `refineStep` is concrete, the cross-config transport (`┬з16.2b` in ChainDescent.lean)
lets us express the forced candidate via a *real* automorphism. A **config-swap** `g` carries the
╧Г-branch config onto the flip-branch config; it forces `╧А_╧Г = ╧А_flip ┬╖ g`, so the candidate is the
`╧А_╧Г`-conjugate of `gтБ╗┬╣`. This reduces the opaque `IsAut candidate adj` to the structural gadget
rank-alignment, isolating the genuine CFI nut (shared with Tier-3a B1 `hwit`): (1) a config-swap
exists, (2) its `╧А_╧Г`-conjugate is an automorphism.

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `ConfigSwap` | 587-599 | A config-swap for decision `(a,b)`: a graph automorphism carrying the ╧Г-branch configuration onto the flip-branch configuration (fixes `╧З╬╣`, sends `╧Г.╧Г` to `(flipPair ╧Г).╧Г`). For CFI, the gadget twist swapping the decided pair. | Structure |
| `configSwap_rankPerm` / `_flip` | The leaf rank perms differ by `g`: `╧А_╧Г = ╧А_flip ┬╖ g` (resp. `╧А_flip = ╧А_╧Г ┬╖ gтБ╗┬╣`), from transport + `vertexRank_comp`. | axiom-light |
| `candidateTwist_eq_conjugate` | 627-637 | **The rank-space reduction.** Given a config-swap `g`, the forced candidate is the `╧А_╧Г`-conjugate of `gтБ╗┬╣` (`candidateTwist = ╧А_╧Г ┬╖ gтБ╗┬╣ ┬╖ ╧А_╧ГтБ╗┬╣`) тАФ the opaque rebasing exposed as a conjugate of a genuine automorphism. | тАФ |
| `isAut_candidateTwist_iff_conjugate` | 639-650 | **The reduction.** `IsAut candidate adj тЖФ IsAut (╧А_╧Г ┬╖ gтБ╗┬╣ ┬╖ ╧А_╧ГтБ╗┬╣) adj` тАФ the rank-space firing obligation is exactly the gadget rank-alignment, the concrete nut shared with Tier-3a B1. | тАФ |

**┬зL.7b тАФ vertex-model soundness (Approach C, the faithful C# model).** A config-swap is a real
graph automorphism, so both branches give the *same canonical leaf* тАФ no rank-alignment needed. This
is the soundness the C# `TwistConstruction` actually uses (it verifies a vertex automorphism, not the
rank rebasing).

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `canonAdj_eq_of_configSwap` | 661-676 | **Equal canonical leaves.** A config-swap implies both branches produce the identical canonical leaf тАФ the vertex-model soundness statement (pruning the flip branch loses nothing), needing no rank-alignment. | тАФ |
| `realizableFlip_of_configSwap` | 678-692 | A config-swap implies `RealizableFlip` (identity witness, since the leaves coincide) тАФ the decision is a genuine `Aut(adj)` symmetry with no rank-alignment obligation. | тАФ |

**┬зL.8 тАФ CFI completeness: config-swap from a swapping automorphism (M1c step 3, the cascade-1b bridge).**
*Where a config-swap comes from.* A swapping automorphism `g` (`g a = b`, `g b = a`) is exactly an
`OrbitPartition adj P S a b` witness specialised to the size-2 decision cell тАФ the cascade oracle's
currency. So linear-oracle CFI completeness reduces to the **shared cascade-1b** obligation
(bounded-depth half `recoverableByDepth_cfi` proved; decision-node-depth bridge open, *not* `GIтИИP`).

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `configSwap_of_aut` | 724-767 | **General constructor (the `hwit` entry point).** *Any* swapping automorphism `g` (`g a = b`, `g b = a`) that fixes `╧З╬╣` and preserves `╧Г.╧Г` *off the flip pair* (`╧Г.╧Г (g v)(g u) = ╧Г.╧Г v u` for `(v,u) тИЙ {(a,b),(b,a)}`) is a `ConfigSwap` тАФ `g` need **not** be a transposition (may move the whole coupled component). Removes the config-swap *packaging* from the open content: once the CFI gadget twist `g` and its off-pair `╧Г`-action are known, the `ConfigSwap` is built with no rank-alignment. | Definition |
| `configSwap_of_swap` | 769-820 | **Closed instance (the `ZтВВ` twin-swap).** A ╧Г-cell-coherent transposition automorphism (`g` swaps `a,b`, fixes the rest and `╧З╬╣`) is a `ConfigSwap` тАФ the simplest genuine abelian decision. Now a thin specialisation of `configSwap_of_aut` (transposition тЗТ off-pair preservation = ╧Г-cell-coherence). | Definition |
| `configSwap_of_twin` | 822-850 | **The twin тЖТ config-swap bridge.** An (adj, ╧Г)-twin decision pair (adjacency-twin on a simple graph plus ╧Г-cell-coherent, `╧З╬╣ a = ╧З╬╣ b`) admits a `ConfigSwap` via the transposition `(a b)` тАФ the linear-oracle analog of `cellsAreOrbits_of_twin_cells`, both oracles firing on the same twin/module class through one shared lemma. Not CFI (which has no twins). | Definition |
| `ConfigSwapRecoverable` | 852-862 | **Decision-node recoverability** (the named cascade-1b obligation for the linear oracle): every leaf decision admits a config-swap. The graph-level analog of `AbelianSufficiencyHolds`; open discharge `configSwapRecoverable_of_cfi` is downstream. | Definition |
| `canonAdj_eq_of_configSwapRecoverable` | 864-875 | **Capstone (pruning soundness).** Config-swap-recoverability implies both branches give the identical canonical leaf at every decision тАФ reducing the oracle's effectiveness to the single `ConfigSwapRecoverable` hypothesis. | тАФ |
| `realizableFlip_of_configSwapRecoverable` | 877-888 | **Capstone (real symmetry).** Config-swap-recoverability implies every leaf decision is a genuine `Aut(adj)` symmetry тАФ vertex-model completeness, no rank-alignment needed. | тАФ |

**┬зL.9 тАФ CFI gadget twist fires the oracle (Phase 6a: wiring the Stage-3 cycle-space flip).** The
Stage-3 gadget flip (`CFI.lean ┬з15`, `IsCFI'.cfiFlipAut`) is now constructed; this section wires it into
`configSwap_of_aut` and reduces `ConfigSwapRecoverable` for CFI to the existence of the right cycle `F`
per decision.

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `configSwap_of_cfiFlipAut` | **The CFI gadget twist is a config-swap** (unconditional bridge). `configSwap_of_aut` instantiated with `g := cfiFlipAut F` (an `Aut(adj)` involution by `isAut_cfiFlipAut`): if the flip swaps `(a,b)`, fixes `╧З╬╣`, and carries `╧Г` off the pair, it is a `ConfigSwap`. The concrete soundness тАФ the vertex-space gadget twist (the C#'s witness) fires the oracle, no rank-alignment. | Definition |
| `CFIGadgetFlippable` | **The named cascade-1b residual.** Every leaf decision admits an even-symmetric cycle `F` whose gadget flip swaps `(a,b)`, fixes `╧З╬╣`, carries `╧Г` off the pair. Commits the CFI witness to the gadget-flip mechanism (matching the C#); the open content is purely `F`'s existence per decision (cascade-1b). | Definition |
| `configSwapRecoverable_of_cfi` | **`ConfigSwapRecoverable` for CFI via the gadget flip.** `CFIGadgetFlippable h тЖТ ConfigSwapRecoverable` тАФ the discharge reduced to its irreducible combinatorial core (the decision-local even cycle's existence). Feeds the capstones тЯ╣ oracle fires on every CFI decision. | тАФ |

Open (not a `sorry`): **`CFIGadgetFlippable`** тАФ that the decision-local even cycle `F` *exists* for every
decision (the flip is built and proven sound; what remains is the cycle through the decision edge, local
to the decided gadget). Its three per-decision obligations (swap `(a,b)`, fix `╧З╬╣`, carry `╧Г` off the
pair) are the descent-coherence content of cascade-1b тАФ the decision-node-depth half, shared with the
cascade oracle, *not* `GIтИИP`.

**┬зL.9 follow-on тАФ the conditions reduced to locality + cell-coherence.** Decouples the gadget-flip
mechanics from the descent's cell structure, so the residual is the cascade-1b shape (F-locality +
cell-coherence), not the opaque `configSwap_of_aut` package.

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `swapsConfig_off_pair_of_local` | **The ╧Г-off-pair reduction (general `g`, reusable).** Any `g` swapping `(a,b)`, fixing decided vertices off `{a,b}`, preserving the decided set and `PтВА`, satisfies the off-pair condition given only **╧Г-cell-coherence** at `(a,b)`. Off-D via `agrees_off` + PтВА-invariance; on-D via the coherence case-analysis. | тАФ |
| `preserves_D_of_involutive_local` | Decided-set preservation for an involutive local swap (`g x тИИ D тЖФ x тИИ D` from `g┬▓=id` + swap + fix-off-`{a,b}`). The `hgD` input above, discharged for the gadget flip. | тАФ |
| `cfiFlipAut_fixes╧З╬╣_of_support` | **The `hg╧З` reduction.** The flip fixes `╧З╬╣` once it does on the F-touched gadgets тАФ Phase-4 locality fixes every `F`-free gadget outright. Reduces global `hg╧З` to ╧З╬╣-coherence on the (small) F-support. | тАФ |
| `configSwap_of_cfiFlipAut_local` | **The reduced bridge.** A `ConfigSwap` from {`F` even+symmetric, swap, **F is D-local**, ╧Г-cell-coherent, `PтВА` Aut-invariant, ╧З╬╣-coherent on F-support} тАФ the three `configSwap_of_aut` conditions discharged via the reductions above. | Definition |
| `CFIGadgetFlippableLocal` | The reduced per-decision predicate: an even-symmetric **D-local** `F` whose flip swaps `(a,b)`, with ╧Г cell-coherent and ╧З╬╣ coherent on the F-support. The conditions are now the descent-coherence / cycle-locality (cascade-1b) facts. | Definition |
| `configSwapRecoverable_of_cfi_local` | `ConfigSwapRecoverable` from `CFIGadgetFlippableLocal` (+ `PтВА` Aut-invariance) тАФ the discharge via the decoupled hypotheses. | тАФ |

**┬зL.9 (C1b.1) тАФ the CFI glue: parity-pair decisions.** Reduces `CFIGadgetFlippableLocal` to the
explicit-edge form, discharging the swap obligation in advance (via C1b.0).

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `CFIParityDecisionFlippable` | The reduced cascade-1b hypothesis: every decision `(a,b)` is the parity-pair of a base edge `{v,w}` (`a = e^{bтВА}_{vтЖТw}`, `b = e^{┬мbтВА}`) admitting an even-symmetric cycle `F` with `{v,w} тИИ F`, D-local, ╧Г/╧З╬╣ cell-coherent. The swap is no longer an obligation (it's `cfiFlipAut_swaps_endpointVertex`); only cycle existence + coherence remain. | Definition |
| `cfiGadgetFlippableLocal_of_parity` | **The C1b.1 glue.** `CFIParityDecisionFlippable тЖТ CFIGadgetFlippableLocal` тАФ the body's two swap conjuncts from `cfiFlipAut_endpointVertex` + `F v w = true`; the rest passes through. Open content narrows to C1b.2 (cycle exists) + C1b.3 (decisions are parity-pairs + coherence). | тАФ |

Transport chain it builds on (ChainDescent.lean `┬з16.2b`): `signature_transport`, `sigKey_transport`,
`refineStep_transport`, `iterate_refineStep_transport`, `warmRefine_transport` тАФ cross-config (two
`(P,╧З)` related by an automorphism), the value-level generalisation of the `*_invariant_of_isAut`
chain, newly provable because `refineStep` is concrete. All axiom-light.

### ┬зL.6 тАФ Relativized completeness (the retargeting)

The general completeness statement ("forced candidate fires whenever the branches are
isomorphic") *provably* cannot close тАФ a realizing aut agrees with the forced candidate only
up to a conjugate of `Aut(adj)` (`rankPerm_comp`), the split-or-Johnson wall *by design*, and
the **same gap the a-priori cascade oracle carries** (`CascadeOracle.lean` ┬з4.3). The fix is
the cascade oracle's **Phase-B move**: relativize completeness to the recoverable/abelian
class and reduce it to orbit recovery. This scaffold names the relativized target and isolates
the one open obligation (`AbelianSufficiencyHolds` on the CFI class тАФ the leaf-level instance
of orbit recovery, the same nut as Tier-3a B1's `hwit`).

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `RankAligned` | 482-490 | The algebraic firing condition: a rank-aligned automorphism exists (`тИГ g тИИ Aut(adj), g ┬╖ ╧А_╧Г = ╧А_flip`). The oracle fires exactly when this holds. | Definition |
| `isAut_candidateTwist_iff_rankAligned` | 492-500 | **Interface.** The forced candidate is an automorphism iff `RankAligned` тАФ the completeness question restated against the named predicate. | тАФ |
| `AbelianSufficiency` | 502-512 | **The per-decision relativized completeness target.** `RealizableFlip тЖТ IsAut candidate`: if the flip is a real symmetry then the forced candidate verifies. False in the non-abelian regime (the wall); the claim to discharge on the abelian/cascade class. | Definition |
| `oracleFires_of_abelianSufficiency` | 514-529 | **Capstone (what suffices).** `AbelianSufficiency` plus a real symmetry implies the oracle fires тАФ the linear-oracle analog of cascade's `cascadeComplete_of_localization`. | тАФ |
| `abelianSufficiency_of_rankPerm_eq` | 531-542 | **Non-vacuous closed instance.** The absorbed decision is abelian-sufficient (candidate `= 1 тИИ Aut` outright) тАФ validates the scaffold against a real instance. | тАФ |
| `AbelianSufficiencyHolds` | 544-552 | The graph-level discharge target: every leaf decision is abelian-sufficient. Open obligation `abelianSufficiencyHolds_of_cfi` is downstream (via `theorem_1_HOR_cfi_oddDeg`, the same nut as Tier-3a B1's `hwit`). | Definition |
| `oracleFires_of_abelianSufficiencyHolds` | 554-568 | **Graph-level capstone.** `AbelianSufficiencyHolds` implies the oracle fires at every leaf decision that is a real symmetry тАФ relativized completeness on the abelian class. | тАФ |

## ChainDescent/Group.lean

Part A (A1тАУA3) of `docs/chain-descent-tier3-tractable-buildout.md` тАФ the group object
the orbit-recovery program deliberately avoided, now needed for Tier-3 vocabulary
(`HтВА тК╡ тАж тК╡ H_k`, quotient graphs). Pure glue over Mathlib group theory + the existing
`IsAut` lemmas; **no `refineStep`** dependency (axioms `[propext, Classical.choice, Quot.sound]`).
A4 (the quotient *graph* `G/H` + cell = quotient-vertex lemma) is **not** here тАФ it is the
medium-risk Mathlib gap gating B1.

### A1 тАФ `Aut(G)` as a group

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `AutGroup adj` | ┬зA1 **The automorphism group.** `{╧А | IsAut ╧А adj}` as a `Subgroup (Equiv.Perm (Fin n))` тАФ the group object Tier-3 vocabulary (`HтВА тК╡ тАж тК╡ H_k`, quotient graphs) is stated over. | Definition |
| `mem_autGroup` | 69-70 | Membership in `AutGroup adj` is exactly `IsAut ╧А adj` (`@[simp]` unfolding). | `@[simp]` |
| `orbitPartition_iff_autGroup` | 72-87 | ┬зA1 **The `OrbitPartition` тЖФ `AutGroup` bridge.** Repackages the bare permutation of the orbit relation as a genuine group element in the pointwise-`S`-stabilizer that preserves `P`, keeping `OrbitPartition` the working object while exposing the group element where the chain needs it. | тАФ |

### A2 тАФ Action on vertices + orbit bridge

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `autGroup_smul` | 96-98 | ┬зA2 The subgroup action's `smul` is permutation application: `g тАв v = (тЖСg) v` (`@[simp]`). | `@[simp]` |
| `mem_orbit_autGroup_iff` | 100-109 | ┬зA2 **Orbit membership, unfolded.** `w` lies in `v`'s `AutGroup`-orbit iff some automorphism sends `v` to `w` (the pure-orbit form, before `OrbitPartition`'s `P`-preservation refinement). | тАФ |
| `mem_orbit_autGroup_iff_orbitPartition` | 111-125 | ┬зA2 **The orbit bridge.** Under `P`-invariance, `v`'s `AutGroup`-orbit coincides with the root relation `OrbitPartition adj P тИЕ` тАФ the group-level reading of the support backbone's root case. | тАФ |

### A3 тАФ Normal subgroup chains

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `LayerChain adj` | ┬зA3 A finite descending chain `AutGroup adj = layer 0 тК╡ тАж тК╡ layer len = тКе`, each layer relatively normal in its predecessor тАФ the `HтВА тК╡ тАж тК╡ H_k` substrate Tier-3a (B1) reasons over. | Structure |
| `LayerChain.trivial` | ┬зA3 **The trivial chain** `AutGroup adj тК╡ тКе` (length 1); witnesses `LayerChain` is inhabited. | Definition |

### A4 тАФ quotient graph + cell = quotient-vertex

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `orbitSetoid adj P S` | ┬зA4 The `Aut_S`-orbit relation `OrbitPartition adj P S` packaged as a `Setoid` from its proved `refl`/`symm`/`trans`. | Definition |
| `OrbitQuotient adj P S` | ┬зA4 **The quotient vertex set** `V(G)/Aut_S` тАФ the vertices of the quotient graph. | `abbrev` |
| `orbitMk` / `orbitMk_eq_iff` | The quotient map `v тЖж тЯжvтЯз`; `orbitMk v = orbitMk w тЖФ OrbitPartition adj P S v w`. | Definition / `Quotient.eq` |
| `cell_iff_orbitMk_eq` | 226-242 | ┬зA4 **The cell = quotient-vertex lemma.** Under `CellsAreOrbits`, two vertices share a 1-WL cell of `(G, S)` iff they are the same quotient vertex тАФ the correspondence B1's cascade-composition induction steps through. | тАФ |
| `QuotientAdjCompatible` | 246-254 | ┬зA4 **Quotient-adjacency compatibility.** The condition that `adj v w` is constant on `Aut_S`-orbit pairs тАФ exactly when a simple induced adjacency on the quotient is well-defined (holds at discreteness, fails for coarser `S`). | Definition |
| `quotientAdj` / `quotientAdj_mk` | The induced adjacency on `OrbitQuotient`, well-defined under `QuotientAdjCompatible` (via `Quotient.liftтВВ`); `quotientAdj h тЯжvтЯз тЯжwтЯз = adj.adj v w` (`rfl`). | Definition / `@[simp]` |
| `quotientAdjCompatible_of_discrete` | 269-280 | ┬зA4 At discreteness the quotient graph is always well-defined (orbits are singletons) тАФ the recursion-bottom anchor, paralleling `cellsAreOrbits_of_discrete`. | тАФ |
| `orbitPartition_empty_iff_orbitRel` | 290-302 | ┬зA4 The root orbit relation `OrbitPartition adj P тИЕ` equals the `AutGroup` `MulAction` orbit relation (under `P`-invariance) тАФ the relational form of the A2 orbit bridge, symmetrised for `orbitRel`. | тАФ |
| `orbitQuotientEquivAutGroup` | 304-312 | ┬зA4 **The root quotient is `V(G)/Aut(G)`.** Under `P`-invariance, `OrbitQuotient adj P тИЕ` is equivalent to the `MulAction` orbit quotient of `AutGroup adj`, tying A4's relational quotient back to A1/A2's group object. | Definition |

| `stabilizer_eq_bot_of_isPretransitive_comm` | 324-342 | **(seal core L1, [exhaustive-obstruction ┬з0.7](../docs/chain-descent-exhaustive-obstruction.md))** A transitive, faithful, **abelian** action is **free**: every point-stabilizer is trivial ("transitive abelian тЯ╣ regular"). The textbook root of "no non-consumed abelian species". | тАФ |
| `existsUnique_smul_of_isPretransitive_comm` | 344-355 | **(seal core L2)** Unique candidate: in a transitive faithful abelian action exactly one group element moves `a` to `b` (existence from transitivity, uniqueness from L1's trivial stabilizer). | тАФ |
| `smul_eq_on_orbit_of_comm` | 357-366 | **(seal core L3 тАФ load-bearing, axiom-free)** Quotient-free, faithfulness-free form: if `g, h` both move `a` to `b` then they agree on the **whole orbit** of `a` (`gтАвc = kтАвb = hтАвc` for `c = kтАвa`). The "unique-candidate-on-the-cell" the linear-oracle harvest reads тАФ holds for an abelian residual even with non-trivial global stabilizers (CFI). | тАФ |
| `aut_agree_on_orbit_of_comm` | 368-382 | **(seal instantiation)** L3 for `AutGroup adj`: an **abelian residual** тЯ╣ two automorphisms both sending `a тЖж b` agree on every `c` in `a`'s orbit, so the decision is determined on its cell (always consumable). | тАФ |
| `not_comm_of_orbit_disagree` | 384-393 | **(seal headline тАФ no non-consumed abelian species)** Contrapositive: a decision `a тЖж b` whose two candidate automorphisms **disagree** on the cell forces a **non-abelian** residual. With the ┬з12 capstone (large primitive non-abelian тЯ╣ Cameron), the only non-consumed symmetry is a Cameron section тАФ the bottom-up, citation-free half of the seal. | тАФ |
| `card_eq_of_isPretransitive_comm` | 404-418 | **(seal Step 4 тАФ order side, [exhaustive-obstruction ┬з0.7](../docs/chain-descent-exhaustive-obstruction.md))** A transitive, faithful, **abelian** action has `Nat.card G = Nat.card ╬▒`: the orbit map `g тЖж gтАвa` is a bijection (free from L1, surjective from transitivity), so order = degree ("abelian primitive тЯ╣ regular, hence small"). | тАФ |
| `not_comm_of_isPretransitive_of_stabilizer_ne_bot` | 420-426 | **(seal Step 4, qualitative)** A transitive faithful action with a **non-trivial** point stabilizer (not regular) is **non-abelian** тАФ direct contrapositive of L1. | тАФ |
| `not_comm_of_isPreprimitive_card_lt` | 428-437 | **(seal Step 4 тАФ the headline: large primitive тЯ╣ non-abelian)** A **preprimitive** faithful action with `Nat.card ╬▒ < Nat.card G` (group strictly larger than its degree) is **non-abelian**, since a transitive abelian action has order = degree. The order-side proof that a primitive abelian group is `Z_p` (never large); closes the bottom-up route's Step 4 with no citation. | тАФ |
## ChainDescent/Cascade.lean

B1 (Tier 3a cascade composition) of `docs/chain-descent-tier3-tractable-buildout.md`,
Phases A + C. Build plan: `docs/chain-descent-tier3a-b1-build-plan.md`. The headline
"depths add" theorem, **conditional on the per-layer transfer** (`LayerStep`, = paper
┬з4.2.5, discharged in the not-yet-built Phase D). Stays on `Fin n` (no quotient
re-typing) by telescoping cumulative individualization sets. Axiom-clean (standard
basis; `refineStep` via `warmRefine`).

### Phase A тАФ interface

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `IsBase adj P T` | **Phase A interface.** `T` is a *base* of the `P`-preserving automorphism group: its pointwise stabilizer is trivial, so the `Aut_T`-orbit relation is equality тАФ the chain's bottom `H_k = {1}`. | Definition |
| `LayerStep adj P T S` | **Phase A interface тАФ the per-layer transfer obligation.** `CellsAreOrbits T тЖТ CellsAreOrbits (T тИк S)`: individualizing the increment `S` brings cells down to `Aut_{TтИкS}`-orbits (paper ┬з4.2.5 transferred to `G`). The contract the composition induction consumes; discharged in Phase D. | Definition |
| (cascade-class predicate) | `RecoverableByDepth adj P bound` (in `CascadeOracle.lean`) тАФ Tier-1 (`recoverableByDepth_cfi`) / Tier-2 (`recoverableByDepth_scheme`) instances already proved. | (existing) |

### Phase C тАФ composition theorem

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `discrete_of_cellsAreOrbits_base` | 83-90 | **(C1) Finish.** At a base `T` where cells already coincide with `Aut_T`-orbits, warm refinement at `T` is `Discrete` тАФ the cascade reaching full canonization. | тАФ |
| `cellsAreOrbits_compose` | 92-105 | **(C2) Composition induction.** From layer 1's unconditional `CellsAreOrbits` at `T 0` and a `LayerStep` at each subsequent layer, `CellsAreOrbits` holds at the final cumulative set `T k`. | тАФ |
| `cumulative_card_le` | 107-113 | **Depths add (cardinality).** The cumulative individualization set `тЛГ_{iтЙдk} S i` has size at most `╬г_{iтЙдk} f i` when each layer is bounded by its depth `f i`. | тАФ |
| `cascadeComposition` | 115-127 | **Theorem 3a (cascade composition) тАФ headline, conditional form.** Cumulative sets with layer-1 recoverability, per-layer transfer steps, and the final set a base тЯ╣ warm refinement at `T k` reaches the discrete partition; with `cumulative_card_le` the cascade depth is `тЙд ╬г fс╡в`. Conditional on the `hstep` obligations (= ┬з4.2.5, Phase D). | тАФ |
| `cascadeComposition_single` | 135-138 | **Single-layer sanity check (k = 0).** One cascade-class layer that is a base reaches discreteness тАФ recovers the Tier-1/Tier-2 orbit-recovery theorems as the composition's base case. | тАФ |

### Phase D тАФ discharging `LayerStep` (the ┬з4.2.5 transfer), intrinsic route

Approach B (build-plan ┬з3): stay on `Fin n`, reduce `LayerStep` to a witness-upgrade via
**set-monotonicity** of warm refinement (reusing `refineStep_iff`); the materialized-quotient
route was rejected (`refineStep` axiomatic, no cross-size API).

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `Refines ╧ЗтВБ ╧ЗтВВ` | `╧ЗтВБ` refines `╧ЗтВВ`: the partition of `╧ЗтВБ` is finer (`╧ЗтВБ a = ╧ЗтВБ b тЖТ ╧ЗтВВ a = ╧ЗтВВ b`). The partition order used for warm-refinement monotonicity. | Definition |
| `signature_refines` | 156-177 | **Crux of warm-refinement monotonicity.** If `╧ЗтВБ` refines `╧ЗтВВ`, equal `╧ЗтВБ`-signatures give equal `╧ЗтВВ`-signatures, since `signature ╧ЗтВВ` is the coarsening of `signature ╧ЗтВБ`. | тАФ |
| `iterate_refineStep_refines` / `warmRefine_refines_initial` | warm refinement monotone in the initial colouring's partition order. | axiom-light |
| `individualizedColouring_refines` | 203-215 | Individualizing a superset gives a finer initial colouring: `T тКЖ T'` тЯ╣ `individualizedColouring n T'` refines `individualizedColouring n T`. | тАФ |
| `warmRefine_indiv_mono` | 217-225 | **Set-monotonicity (the payoff).** Same `(T тИк S)`-cell тЯ╣ same `T`-cell: 1-WL is monotone in the individualization set. The load-bearing lemma the docs had mis-cited as `warmRefine_refines`. | тАФ |
| `WitnessUpgrade adj P T S` | **The genuine ┬з4.2.5 content.** For `v, w` in the same `Aut_T`-orbit and the same `(T тИк S)`-cell, the orbit relation upgrades to `Aut_{TтИкS}`. The Phase-D interface predicate. | Definition |
| `layerStep_of_witnessUpgrade` | 239-246 | **The reduction тАФ where Phase C meets the per-layer content.** A `WitnessUpgrade` discharges a `LayerStep`, via set-monotonicity then `CellsAreOrbits T` then the upgrade. | тАФ |
| `layerStep_empty` / `layerStep_subset` / `layerStep_of_cellsAreOrbits` / `layerStep_of_discrete` | Trivial real instances: no-op layer (`S = тИЕ`), `S тКЖ T`, independently-recoverable target, and the discretizing recursion-bottom. | axiom-light |
| `witnessUpgrade_of_pathFixing` | 271-286 | **Bridge to harvested generators.** If every same-orbit, same-cell pair admits a `P`-preserving automorphism whose support avoids `T тИк S` (fixes the committed path) and sends `v тЖж w`, the witness-upgrade holds тАФ exactly what the cascade/linear oracles produce. | тАФ |

### Step 5 тАФ the synthesis (Theorem 3a reduced to harvested generators)

| Name | Description | Notes |
|------|-------------|-------|
| `cascadeComposition_pathFixing` | 305-326 | **Theorem 3a, reduced to harvested path-fixing generators.** Cumulative sets by increments, layer-1 recoverable, every layer's residual symmetry realized by path-fixing automorphisms (`hwit`), and the final set a base тЯ╣ discrete warm refinement at `T k`. Reduces all of Theorem 3a to the single hypothesis of per-layer path-fixing witness existence. | тАФ |
| `cascadeComposition_twoLayer` | 328-343 | **Smallest genuine composition.** An outer cascade-class layer at `TтВА`, an inner path-fixing layer with increment `S`, and the union a base тЯ╣ discreteness тАФ the `CFI(scheme)` / `Scheme(CFI)` shape. | тАФ |

**Phase 6b тАФ CFI gadget flips discharge the Tier-3a `hwit`.** The Stage-3 gadget flip (`CFI.lean ┬з15`)
discharges `cascadeComposition_pathFixing`'s `hwit` for a CFI layering, conditional only on the per-layer
existence of committed-set-avoiding gadget flips (the cascade-1b content).

Recovery of the coarser action on blocks only тАФ strictly weaker than full orbit recovery, and the part of Route B that survives when the whole residual does not recover. Class-agnostic (any `╬▓`, any `adj`/`P`). | тАФ |
| `hfiber_of_fiberRealizers` | 1457-1469 | **(Route B `hfiber` supplier тАФ the smaller fiber interface)** Discharges the within-block interface `hfiber` from **fiber realizers**: residual auts in `gens` exactly realizing every *same-block* orbit pair (`╬▓ u = ╬▓ w тЖТ h u = w`). Recovery of the smaller within-block (`|B| < n`) action only тАФ the second constituent of the imprimitive decomposition. Class-agnostic. | тАФ |
| `hfiber_of_fiberVisibleRealizers` | 1471-1491 | **(Route B fiber half тАФ `hfiber` from within-block visible realizers, Approach A)** Refinement-computable form of `hfiber_of_fiberRealizers`: the harvest need only realize same-`warmRefine`-cell pairs *within a block* (`╬▓ u = ╬▓ w`), and `hfiber` follows (orbits refine cells, `OrbitPartition.subset_warmRefine`). **Strictly weaker than whole-graph recovery** тАФ satisfiable exactly when *within each block* cells = orbits (the fiber recovers), even when globally cells тКЛ orbits (e.g. Shrikhande, whose 1-WL merges happen across blocks). The fiber half of the per-level quotient/fiber split; the quotient half (`hreach` from block-orbit recovery) needs a block-level 1-WL (next step). | тАФ |
| `hreach_of_quotientVisibleRealizers` | 1493-1517 | **(Route B quotient half from VISIBLE realizers тАФ the named G2-A "next step")** The quotient analogue of `hfiber_of_fiberVisibleRealizers`, completing the refinement-computable supply for *both* halves of the block decomposition. From a visible block-move hypothesis (`warmRefine{T} b = warmRefine{T} w тЖТ тИГ ╧Г тИИ gens, ResidualAut T ╧Г тИз ╬▓(╧Гb)=╬▓w` тАФ `╧Г` lands `b` in `w`'s **block**, not at `w`), supplies `hreach`: orbits refine cells (`OrbitPartition.subset_warmRefine`) so an orbit pair is a cell pair. Non-vacuity: same-block cell pairs free (`╧Г=id`); the content is *cross-block* same-cell pairs = recovery of the (coarser) **block action** (block-level 1-WL). Discharges the shallow-phase (quotient) coverage for the imprimitive case. | тАФ |
| `reachesRigid_of_blockVisibleDecomposition` | 1519-1545 | **(imprimitive recovery from a fully refinement-computable block decomposition тАФ shallow-phase discharge)** Both halves now visible: combines `hreach_of_quotientVisibleRealizers` (quotient/shallow) + `hfiber_of_fiberVisibleRealizers` (fiber/deep) through `reachesRigid_of_blockDecomposition` to reproduce `closure (gensAt тАж S) = StabilizerAt adj P S` from a **non-vacuous, refinement-computable** decomposition, no sub-scheme materialized. Completes the Route B reduction with *both* coverage interfaces keyed on visible realizers (matching `SchemeRecovered`'s non-vacuity). Residual carried content = the two visible hypotheses `hqvis`/`hfvis` (whether the quotient + fiber recover, i.e. their block-level/within-block WL-dimension) тАФ the substrate-conditional unit, localized to the two smaller constituents. Axiom-clean. | тАФ |
| `blockHarvest_of_realizers` | 1547-1564 | **(Route B subsumption / non-vacuity floor)** Full orbit realizers (`g b = w` for every orbit pair) supply **both** `hreach` and `hfiber`, for **any** `╬▓` (left unused тАФ an exact realizer is a fortiori block-accurate and within-block-exact). So any whole-residual-recoverable class satisfies the Route B interfaces; the decomposition's independent value is strictly the regime where quotient/fiber recover but the whole does not. Built from `hreach_of_quotientRealizers` + `hfiber_of_fiberRealizers`. | тАФ |
| `blockHarvest_of_visibleRecovery` | 1566-1585 | **(Route B witness supplier тАФ recovery + visible realizers тЯ╣ both interfaces)** The refinement-computable form: `CellsAreOrbits` recovery at every level + a path-fixing realizer for every visible cell-mate supply both `hreach` and `hfiber` (any `╬▓`), via `orbitRealizers_iff_visibleRealizers_of_cellsAreOrbits` + `blockHarvest_of_realizers`. The Route B analogue of `noFusion_of_visibleRecovery`: the metric/DRG (`recoverableByDepth_pPolynomial`) and CFI (`recoverableByDepth_cfi`) recovery witnesses plug straight in to discharge the imprimitive branch on the whole recoverable class. | тАФ |
| `coversOrbits_of_residualInvolutive` | 1587-1605 | **(A2-complete) De-classed coverage тАФ `CoversOrbits` from an exponent-2 residual.** If the residual is involutive (`ResidualInvolutive`) and `gens` contains every involutive residual automorphism (what the leaf-collision harvest supplies), `CoversOrbits adj P gens bs S` holds. **Now a corollary of `coversOrbits_of_realizers`** (the general non-abelian form): `orbitPartition_swap_of_involutive` supplies the involution realizer for each orbit-mate. | `movedStep` | 2625-2629 | Leg A тАФ one round of the moved-vertex closure: individualize a moved vertex if one exists, else stay. Extensive; strictly grows until the residual is trivial (a base). | Definition, `noncomputable` |
| `exists_isBase_saturated` | 2640-2657 | **Leg A тАФ the general support induction (every graph reaches a base).** Individualizing moved vertices from any `SтВА` reaches a base `S* тКЗ SтВА` (trivial residual) within `тЙд n тИТ |SтВА|` rounds, via the `Saturation` engine тАФ holding for every graph (CFI, schemes, rigid alike). | тАФ |
| `MovedAt.anti` | 2670-2679 | **Moved-set anti-monotonicity.** A residual automorphism fixing `S` also fixes any `SтВА тКЖ S`, so a vertex moved at `S` is already moved at `SтВА` тАФ the moved-set shrinks as the individualized set grows, which makes it a saturation bound. | тАФ |

## ChainDescent/CoherentConfig.lean

The **general (multi-fiber) coherent-configuration substrate** тАФ Stage 0/1 of the general-CC
separability build (`docs/chain-descent-general-cc-separability.md`; Stage-0 decision + increment log
in its ┬з8). Lands the `CoherentConfig` type (colour-function presentation, fibers *derived*), the
homogeneous coercion, the general-CC `AlgIso`/`Separable` (the ┬зS.17 widening the Stage-1.3 soundness
gate demanded), the probe-validated Thm 4.1 hypothesis predicates (`Theorem41ConditionsProbe.cs`),
the cited `Theorem41Statement` (the staging-fallback carry), and the point extension as a universal
property тАФ **plus its ┬зCC.8 construction (Stage 1.2, 2026-06-12)**: the coherent closure
`pointExtension X T` via a pair-refinement saturation (setoid `pairStep`, representative-indexed
counts, `n┬▓`-round pigeonhole), discharging `IsPointExtension` constructively
(`isPointExtension_pointExtension` / `exists_isPointExtension` / `isPointExtension_unique`).
Axiom-clean `[propext, Classical.choice, Quot.sound]`, no `sorry`.

| Name | Line | Description | Notes |

| `CoherentConfig` | 48-74 | **The general (multi-fiber) coherent configuration** on `Fin n`, by its colour function `relOf : Fin n тЖТ Fin n тЖТ Fin rank` + four axioms (classes nonempty, transpose well-defined, reflexive classes purely diagonal, intersection numbers constant). The central missing object the live build creates; the point extension `X_T` (non-homogeneous) is why it exists. | Structure |

| `CoherentConfig.pairCount_swap` | 556-575 | Counts of the swapped pair under a swap-stable partition are a pure reindexing: `pairCount s v u x y = pairCount s u v y.swap x.swap` тАФ the combinatorial core of the closure's transpose axiom. | тАФ |
